class=\"pl-cce\"\u003e\\\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e        # Check if a title was -h\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003efabric -h\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"Usage:\n  fabric [OPTIONS]\n\nApplication Options:\n  -p, --pattern=                    Choose a pattern from the available patterns\n  -v, --variable=                   Values for pattern variables, e.g. -v=#role:expert -v=#points:30\n  -C, --context=                    Choose a context from the available contexts\n      --session=                    Choose a session from the available sessions\n  -a, --attachment=                 Attachment path or URL (e.g. for OpenAI image recognition messages)\n  -S, --setup                       Run setup for all reconfigurable parts of fabric\n  -t, --temperature=                Set temperature (default: 0.7)\n  -T, --topp=                       Set top P (default: 0.9)\n  -s, --stream                      Stream\n  -P, --presencepenalty=            Set presence penalty (default: 0.0)\n  -r, --raw                         Use the defaults of the model without sending chat options (like\n                                    temperature etc.) and use the user role instead of the system role for\n                                    patterns.\n  -F, --frequencypenalty=           Set frequency penalty (default: 0.0)\n  -l, --listpatterns                List all patterns\n  -L, --listmodels                  List all available models\n  -x, --listcontexts                List all contexts\n  -X, --listsessions                List all sessions\n  -U, --updatepatterns              Update patterns\n  -c, --copy                        Copy to clipboard\n  -m, --model=                      Choose model\n      --modelContextLength=         Model context length (only affects ollama)\n  -o, --output=                     Output to file\n      --output-session              Output the entire session (also a temporary one) to the output file\n  -n, --latest=                     Number of latest patterns to list (default: 0)\n  -d, --changeDefaultModel          Change default model\n  -y, --youtube=                    YouTube video or play list \u0026quot;URL\u0026quot; to grab transcript, comments from it\n                                    and send to chat or print it put to the console and store it in the\n                                    output file\n      --playlist                    Prefer playlist over video if both ids are present in the URL\n      --transcript                  Grab transcript from YouTube video and send to chat (it is used per\n                                    default).\n      --transcript-with-timestamps  Grab transcript from YouTube video with timestamps and send to chat\n      --comments                    Grab comments from YouTube video and send to chat\n      --metadata                    Output video metadata\n  -g, --language= \u003cem\u003ePatterns\u003c/em\u003e are different than most prompts you'll see.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFirst, we use \u003ccode\u003eMarkdown\u003c/code\u003e to help ensure maximum readability and editability\u003c/strong\u003e. can\nbe used in addition to the basic patterns.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSee the \u003ca href=\"https://arxiv.org/pdf/2502.18600\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eThinking Faster by Writing No problem!\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFabric now supports a dedicated custom patterns directory that keeps your personal patterns separate from the built-in ones. This means your custom patterns won't be overwritten when you update Fabric's built-in patterns.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" \u003ccode\u003epbpaste\u003c/code\u003e is not available on Windows or Linux, but there are alternatives.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eOn Windows, you can use the PowerShell command \u003ccode\u003eGet-Clipboard\u003c/code\u003e from a PowerShell command prompt. If you are using classic PowerShell, edit the file \u003ccode\u003e~\\Documents\\WindowsPowerShell\\.profile.ps1\u003c/code\u003e, or if you are using PowerShell Core, edit \u003ccode\u003e~\\Documents\\PowerShell\\.profile.ps1\u003c/code\u003e and add the alias,\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"Set-Alias pbpaste Get-Clipboard\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eSet-Alias\u003c/span\u003e pbpaste \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eGet-Clipboard\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eOn Linux, you can use \u003ccode\u003exclip -selection clipboard -o\u003c/code\u003e to paste from the clipboard. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>fabric</code> is an open-source framework for augmenting humans using AI.</h4><a id="user-content-fabric-is-an-open-source-framework-for-augmenting-humans-using-ai" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: fabric is an open-source framework for augmenting humans using AI." href="#fabric-is-an-open-source-framework-for-augmenting-humans-using-ai"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What and why</h2><a id="user-content-what-and-why" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What and why" href="#what-and-why"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Since the start of modern AI in late 2022 we've seen an <strong><em>extraordinary</em></strong> number of AI applications for accomplishing tasks. There are thousands of websites, chat-bots, mobile apps, and other interfaces for using all the different AI out there.</p>
<p dir="auto">It's all really exciting and powerful, but <em>it's not easy to integrate this functionality into our lives.</em></p>
<div dir="auto">
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">In other words, AI doesn't have a capabilities problem—it has an <em>integration</em> problem.</h4><a id="user-content-in-other-words-ai-doesnt-have-a-capabilities-problemit-has-an-integration-problem" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: In other words, AI doesn't have a capabilities problem—it has an integration problem." href="#in-other-words-ai-doesnt-have-a-capabilities-problemit-has-an-integration-problem"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
</div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Fabric was created to address this by creating and organizing the fundamental units of AI—the prompts themselves!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Fabric organizes prompts by real-world task, allowing people to create, collect, and organize their most important AI solutions in a single place for use in their favorite tools. And if you're command-line focused, you can use Fabric itself as the interface!</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Intro videos</h2><a id="user-content-intro-videos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Intro videos" href="#intro-videos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Keep in mind that many of these were recorded when Fabric was Python-based, so remember to use the current <a href="#installation">install instructions</a> below.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Navigation</h2><a id="user-content-navigation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Navigation" href="#navigation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Updates</h2><a id="user-content-updates" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Updates" href="#updates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-note" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-info mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 7h1a.75.75 0 0 1 .75.75v2.75h.25a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-2a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5h.25v-2h-.25a.75.75 0 0 1-.75-.75ZM8 6a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Z"></path></svg>Note</p>
<p dir="auto">July 4, 2025</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Web Search</strong>: Fabric now supports web search for Anthropic and OpenAI models using the <code>--search</code> and <code>--search-location</code> flags. This replaces the previous plugin-based search, so you may want to remove the old <code>ANTHROPIC_WEB_SEARCH_TOOL_*</code> variables from your <code>~/.config/fabric/.env</code> file.</li>
<li><strong>Image Generation</strong>: Fabric now has powerful image generation capabilities with OpenAI.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Generate images from text prompts and save them using <code>--image-file</code>.</li>
<li>Edit existing images by providing an input image with <code>--attachment</code>.</li>
<li>Control image <code>size</code>, <code>quality</code>, <code>compression</code>, and <code>background</code> with the new <code>--image-*</code> flags.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">June 17, 2025</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Fabric now supports Perplexity AI. Configure it by using <code>fabric -S</code> to add your Perplexity AI API Key,
and then try:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fabric -m sonar-pro &quot;What is the latest world news?&quot;"><pre>fabric -m sonar-pro <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>What is the latest world news?<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">June 11, 2025</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Fabric's YouTube transcription now needs <code>yt-dlp</code> to be installed. Make sure to install the latest
version (2025.06.09 as of this note). The YouTube API key is only needed for comments (the <code>--comments</code> flag)
and metadata extraction (the <code>--metadata</code> flag).</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Philosophy</h2><a id="user-content-philosophy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Philosophy" href="#philosophy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">AI isn't a thing; it's a <em>magnifier</em> of a thing. And that thing is <strong>human creativity</strong>.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">We believe the purpose of technology is to help humans flourish, so when we talk about AI we start with the <strong>human</strong> problems we want to solve.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Breaking problems into components</h3><a id="user-content-breaking-problems-into-components" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Breaking problems into components" href="#breaking-problems-into-components"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Our approach is to break problems into individual pieces (see below) and then apply AI to them one at a time. See below for some examples.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/assets/50654/31997394-85a9-40c2-879b-b347e4701f06"><img width="2000" alt="augmented_challenges" src="https://github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/assets/50654/31997394-85a9-40c2-879b-b347e4701f06" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Too many prompts</h3><a id="user-content-too-many-prompts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Too many prompts" href="#too-many-prompts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Prompts are good for this, but the biggest challenge I faced in 2023——which still exists today—is <strong>the sheer number of AI prompts out there</strong>. We all have prompts that are useful, but it's hard to discover new ones, know if they are good or not, <em>and manage different versions of the ones we like</em>.</p>
<p dir="auto">One of <code>fabric</code>'s primary features is helping people collect and integrate prompts, which we call <em>Patterns</em>, into various parts of their lives.</p>
<p dir="auto">Fabric has Patterns for all sorts of life and work activities, including:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Extracting the most interesting parts of YouTube videos and podcasts</li>
<li>Writing an essay in your own voice with just an idea as an input</li>
<li>Summarizing opaque academic papers</li>
<li>Creating perfectly matched AI art prompts for a piece of writing</li>
<li>Rating the quality of content to see if you want to read/watch the whole thing</li>
<li>Getting summaries of long, boring content</li>
<li>Explaining code to you</li>
<li>Turning bad documentation into usable documentation</li>
<li>Creating social media posts from any content input</li>
<li>And a million more…</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To install Fabric, you can use the latest release binaries or install it from the source.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Get Latest Release Binaries</h3><a id="user-content-get-latest-release-binaries" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Get Latest Release Binaries" href="#get-latest-release-binaries"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">macOS (arm64)</h4><a id="user-content-macos-arm64" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: macOS (arm64)" href="#macos-arm64"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Linux (amd64)</h4><a id="user-content-linux-amd64" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Linux (amd64)" href="#linux-amd64"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Linux (arm64)</h4><a id="user-content-linux-arm64" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Linux (arm64)" href="#linux-arm64"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Using package managers</h3><a id="user-content-using-package-managers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Using package managers" href="#using-package-managers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE:</strong> using Homebrew or the Arch Linux package managers makes <code>fabric</code> available as <code>fabric-ai</code>, so add
the following alias to your shell startup files to account for this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="alias fabric='fabric-ai'"><pre><span class="pl-c1">alias</span> fabric=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>fabric-ai<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">macOS (Homebrew)</h4><a id="user-content-macos-homebrew" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: macOS (Homebrew)" href="#macos-homebrew"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Arch Linux (AUR)</h4><a id="user-content-arch-linux-aur" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Arch Linux (AUR)" href="#arch-linux-aur"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">From Source</h3><a id="user-content-from-source" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: From Source" href="#from-source"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To install Fabric, <a href="https://go.dev/doc/install" rel="nofollow">make sure Go is installed</a>, and then run the following command.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Install Fabric directly from the repo
go install github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/cmd/fabric@latest"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install Fabric directly from the repo</span>
go install github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/cmd/fabric@latest</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment Variables</h3><a id="user-content-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment Variables" href="#environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You may need to set some environment variables in your <code>~/.bashrc</code> on linux or <code>~/.zshrc</code> file on mac to be able to run the <code>fabric</code> command. Here is an example of what you can add:</p>
<p dir="auto">For Intel based macs or linux</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Golang environment variables
export GOROOT=/usr/local/go
export GOPATH=$HOME/go

# Update PATH to include GOPATH and GOROOT binaries
export PATH=$GOPATH/bin:$GOROOT/bin:$HOME/.local/bin:$PATH"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Golang environment variables</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> GOROOT=/usr/local/go
<span class="pl-k">export</span> GOPATH=<span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/go

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Update PATH to include GOPATH and GOROOT binaries</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> PATH=<span class="pl-smi">$GOPATH</span>/bin:<span class="pl-smi">$GOROOT</span>/bin:<span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/.local/bin:<span class="pl-smi">$PATH</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">for Apple Silicon based macs</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Golang environment variables
export GOROOT=$(brew --prefix go)/libexec
export GOPATH=$HOME/go
export PATH=$GOPATH/bin:$GOROOT/bin:$HOME/.local/bin:$PATH"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Golang environment variables</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> GOROOT=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>brew --prefix go<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>/libexec
<span class="pl-k">export</span> GOPATH=<span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/go
<span class="pl-k">export</span> PATH=<span class="pl-smi">$GOPATH</span>/bin:<span class="pl-smi">$GOROOT</span>/bin:<span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/.local/bin:<span class="pl-smi">$PATH</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Setup</h3><a id="user-content-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Setup" href="#setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Now run the following command</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Run the setup to set up your directories and keys
fabric --setup"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run the setup to set up your directories and keys</span>
fabric --setup</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If everything works you are good to go.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Add aliases for all patterns</h3><a id="user-content-add-aliases-for-all-patterns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Add aliases for all patterns" href="#add-aliases-for-all-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In order to add aliases for all your patterns and use them directly as commands ie. <code>summarize</code> instead of <code>fabric --pattern summarize</code>
You can add the following to your <code>.zshrc</code> or <code>.bashrc</code> file.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Loop through all files in the ~/.config/fabric/patterns directory
for pattern_file in $HOME/.config/fabric/patterns/*; do
    # Get the base name of the file (i.e., remove the directory path)
    pattern_name=$(basename &quot;$pattern_file&quot;)

    # Create an alias in the form: alias pattern_name=&quot;fabric --pattern pattern_name&quot;
    alias_command=&quot;alias $pattern_name='fabric --pattern $pattern_name'&quot;

    # Evaluate the alias command to add it to the current shell
    eval &quot;$alias_command&quot;
done

yt() {
    if [ &quot;$#&quot; -eq 0 ] || [ &quot;$#&quot; -gt 2 ]; then
        echo &quot;Usage: yt [-t | --timestamps] youtube-link&quot;
        echo &quot;Use the '-t' flag to get the transcript with timestamps.&quot;
        return 1
    fi

    transcript_flag=&quot;--transcript&quot;
    if [ &quot;$1&quot; = &quot;-t&quot; ] || [ &quot;$1&quot; = &quot;--timestamps&quot; ]; then
        transcript_flag=&quot;--transcript-with-timestamps&quot;
        shift
    fi
    local video_link=&quot;$1&quot;
    fabric -y &quot;$video_link&quot; $transcript_flag
}"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Loop through all files in the ~/.config/fabric/patterns directory</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">pattern_file</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/.config/fabric/patterns/<span class="pl-k">*</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Get the base name of the file (i.e., remove the directory path)</span>
    pattern_name=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>basename <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$pattern_file</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Create an alias in the form: alias pattern_name="fabric --pattern pattern_name"</span>
    alias_command=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>alias <span class="pl-smi">$pattern_name</span>='fabric --pattern <span class="pl-smi">$pattern_name</span>'<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Evaluate the alias command to add it to the current shell</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">eval</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$alias_command</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">done</span>

<span class="pl-en">yt</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$#</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-eq</span> 0 ] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$#</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-gt</span> 2 ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Usage: yt [-t | --timestamps] youtube-link<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Use the '-t' flag to get the transcript with timestamps.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1
    <span class="pl-k">fi</span>

    transcript_flag=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>--transcript<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>-t<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>--timestamps<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
        transcript_flag=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>--transcript-with-timestamps<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        <span class="pl-c1">shift</span>
    <span class="pl-k">fi</span>
    <span class="pl-k">local</span> video_link=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    fabric -y <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$video_link</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-smi">$transcript_flag</span>
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can add the below code for the equivalent aliases inside PowerShell by running <code>notepad $PROFILE</code> inside a PowerShell window:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Path to the patterns directory
$patternsPath = Join-Path $HOME &quot;.config/fabric/patterns&quot;
foreach ($patternDir in Get-ChildItem -Path $patternsPath -Directory) {
    $patternName = $patternDir.Name

    # Dynamically define a function for each pattern
    $functionDefinition = @&quot;
function $patternName {
    [CmdletBinding()]
    param(
        [Parameter(ValueFromPipeline = `$true)]
        [string] `$InputObject,

        [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments = `$true)]
        [String[]] `$patternArgs
    )

    begin {
        # Initialize an array to collect pipeline input
        `$collector = @()
    }

    process {
        # Collect pipeline input objects
        if (`$InputObject) {
            `$collector += `$InputObject
        }
    }

    end {
        # Join all pipeline input into a single string, separated by newlines
        `$pipelineContent = `$collector -join &quot;`n&quot;

        # If there's pipeline input, include it in the call to fabric
        if (`$pipelineContent) {
            `$pipelineContent | fabric --pattern $patternName `$patternArgs
        } else {
            # No pipeline input; just call fabric with the additional args
            fabric --pattern $patternName `$patternArgs
        }
    }
}
&quot;@
    # Add the function to the current session
    Invoke-Expression $functionDefinition
}

# Define the 'yt' function as well
function yt {
    [CmdletBinding()]
    param(
        [Parameter()]
        [Alias(&quot;timestamps&quot;)]
        [switch]$t,

        [Parameter(Position = 0, ValueFromPipeline = $true)]
        [string]$videoLink
    )

    begin {
        $transcriptFlag = &quot;--transcript&quot;
        if ($t) {
            $transcriptFlag = &quot;--transcript-with-timestamps&quot;
        }
    }

    process {
        if (-not $videoLink) {
            Write-Error &quot;Usage: yt [-t | --timestamps] youtube-link&quot;
            return
        }
    }

    end {
        if ($videoLink) {
            # Execute and allow output to flow through the pipeline
            fabric -y $videoLink $transcriptFlag
        }
    }
}"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Path to the patterns directory</span>
<span class="pl-smi">$patternsPath</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Join-Path</span> <span class="pl-c1">$HOME</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>.config/fabric/patterns<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">foreach</span> (<span class="pl-smi">$patternDir</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">Get-ChildItem</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-smi">$patternsPath</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Directory) {
    <span class="pl-smi">$patternName</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">$patternDir<span class="pl-smi">.Name</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Dynamically define a function for each pattern</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">$functionDefinition</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">@"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">function <span class="pl-smi">$patternName</span> {</span>
<span class="pl-s">    [CmdletBinding()]</span>
<span class="pl-s">    param(</span>
<span class="pl-s">        [Parameter(ValueFromPipeline = <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>true)]</span>
<span class="pl-s">        [string] <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>InputObject,</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">        [Parameter(ValueFromRemainingArguments = <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>true)]</span>
<span class="pl-s">        [String[]] <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>patternArgs</span>
<span class="pl-s">    )</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    begin {</span>
<span class="pl-s">        # Initialize an array to collect pipeline input</span>
<span class="pl-s">        <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>collector = @()</span>
<span class="pl-s">    }</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    process {</span>
<span class="pl-s">        # Collect pipeline input objects</span>
<span class="pl-s">        if (<span class="pl-cce">`$</span>InputObject) {</span>
<span class="pl-s">            <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>collector += <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>InputObject</span>
<span class="pl-s">        }</span>
<span class="pl-s">    }</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    end {</span>
<span class="pl-s">        # Join all pipeline input into a single string, separated by newlines</span>
<span class="pl-s">        <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>pipelineContent = <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>collector -join "<span class="pl-cce">`n</span>"</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">        # If there's pipeline input, include it in the call to fabric</span>
<span class="pl-s">        if (<span class="pl-cce">`$</span>pipelineContent) {</span>
<span class="pl-s">            <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>pipelineContent | fabric --pattern <span class="pl-smi">$patternName</span> <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>patternArgs</span>
<span class="pl-s">        } else {</span>
<span class="pl-s">            # No pipeline input; just call fabric with the additional args</span>
<span class="pl-s">            fabric --pattern <span class="pl-smi">$patternName</span> <span class="pl-cce">`$</span>patternArgs</span>
<span class="pl-s">        }</span>
<span class="pl-s">    }</span>
<span class="pl-s">}</span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"@</span></span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Add the function to the current session</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">Invoke-Expression</span> <span class="pl-smi">$functionDefinition</span>
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Define the 'yt' function as well</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">yt</span> {
    [<span class="pl-c1">CmdletBinding</span>()]
    <span class="pl-k">param</span>(
        [<span class="pl-c1">Parameter</span>()]
        [<span class="pl-c1">Alias</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>timestamps<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)]
        [<span class="pl-k">switch</span>]<span class="pl-smi">$t</span><span class="pl-k">,</span>

        [<span class="pl-c1">Parameter</span>(<span class="pl-v">Position</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-k">,</span> <span class="pl-v">ValueFromPipeline</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">$true</span>)]
        [<span class="pl-k">string</span>]<span class="pl-smi">$videoLink</span>
    )

    <span class="pl-k">begin</span> {
        <span class="pl-smi">$transcriptFlag</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>--transcript<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">$t</span>) {
            <span class="pl-smi">$transcriptFlag</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>--transcript-with-timestamps<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
        }
    }

    <span class="pl-k">process</span> {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-k">-not</span> <span class="pl-smi">$videoLink</span>) {
            <span class="pl-c1">Write-Error</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Usage: yt [-t | --timestamps] youtube-link<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
            <span class="pl-k">return</span>
        }
    }

    <span class="pl-k">end</span> {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-smi">$videoLink</span>) {
            <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Execute and allow output to flow through the pipeline</span>
            fabric <span class="pl-k">-</span>y <span class="pl-smi">$videoLink</span> <span class="pl-smi">$transcriptFlag</span>
        }
    }
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This also creates a <code>yt</code> alias that allows you to use <code>yt https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4b0iet22VIk</code> to get transcripts, comments, and metadata.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Save your files in markdown using aliases</h4><a id="user-content-save-your-files-in-markdown-using-aliases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Save your files in markdown using aliases" href="#save-your-files-in-markdown-using-aliases"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If in addition to the above aliases you would like to have the option to save the output to your favorite markdown note vault like Obsidian then instead of the above add the following to your <code>.zshrc</code> or <code>.bashrc</code> file:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Define the base directory for Obsidian notes
obsidian_base=&quot;/path/to/obsidian&quot;

# Loop through all files in the ~/.config/fabric/patterns directory
for pattern_file in ~/.config/fabric/patterns/*; do
    # Get the base name of the file (i.e., remove the directory path)
    pattern_name=$(basename &quot;$pattern_file&quot;)

    # Remove any existing alias with the same name
    unalias &quot;$pattern_name&quot; 2&gt;/dev/null

    # Define a function dynamically for each pattern
    eval &quot;
    $pattern_name() {
        local title=\$1
        local date_stamp=\$(date +'%Y-%m-%d')
        local output_path=\&quot;\$obsidian_base/\${date_stamp}-\${title}.md\&quot;

        # Check if a title was provided
        if [ -n \&quot;\$title\&quot; ]; then
            # If a title is provided, use the output path
            fabric --pattern \&quot;$pattern_name\&quot; -o \&quot;\$output_path\&quot;
        else
            # If no title is provided, use --stream
            fabric --pattern \&quot;$pattern_name\&quot; --stream
        fi
    }
    &quot;
done"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Define the base directory for Obsidian notes</span>
obsidian_base=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/path/to/obsidian<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Loop through all files in the ~/.config/fabric/patterns directory</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">pattern_file</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.config/fabric/patterns/<span class="pl-k">*</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Get the base name of the file (i.e., remove the directory path)</span>
    pattern_name=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>basename <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$pattern_file</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Remove any existing alias with the same name</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">unalias</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$pattern_name</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Define a function dynamically for each pattern</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">eval</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">    <span class="pl-smi">$pattern_name</span>() {</span>
<span class="pl-s">        local title=<span class="pl-cce">\$</span>1</span>
<span class="pl-s">        local date_stamp=<span class="pl-cce">\$</span>(date +'%Y-%m-%d')</span>
<span class="pl-s">        local output_path=<span class="pl-cce">\"\$</span>obsidian_base/<span class="pl-cce">\$</span>{date_stamp}-<span class="pl-cce">\$</span>{title}.md<span class="pl-cce">\"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">        # Check if a title was provided</span>
<span class="pl-s">        if [ -n <span class="pl-cce">\"\$</span>title<span class="pl-cce">\"</span> ]; then</span>
<span class="pl-s">            # If a title is provided, use the output path</span>
<span class="pl-s">            fabric --pattern <span class="pl-cce">\"</span><span class="pl-smi">$pattern_name</span><span class="pl-cce">\"</span> -o <span class="pl-cce">\"\$</span>output_path<span class="pl-cce">\"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">        else</span>
<span class="pl-s">            # If no title is provided, use --stream</span>
<span class="pl-s">            fabric --pattern <span class="pl-cce">\"</span><span class="pl-smi">$pattern_name</span><span class="pl-cce">\"</span> --stream</span>
<span class="pl-s">        fi</span>
<span class="pl-s">    }</span>
<span class="pl-s">    <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will allow you to use the patterns as aliases like in the above for example <code>summarize</code> instead of <code>fabric --pattern summarize --stream</code>, however if you pass in an extra argument like this <code>summarize "my_article_title"</code> your output will be saved in the destination that you set in <code>obsidian_base="/path/to/obsidian"</code> in the following format <code>YYYY-MM-DD-my_article_title.md</code> where the date gets autogenerated for you.
You can tweak the date format by tweaking the <code>date_stamp</code> format.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Migration</h3><a id="user-content-migration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Migration" href="#migration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you have the Legacy (Python) version installed and want to migrate to the Go version, here's how you do it. It's basically two steps: 1) uninstall the Python version, and 2) install the Go version.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Uninstall Legacy Fabric
pipx uninstall fabric

# Clear any old Fabric aliases
(check your .bashrc, .zshrc, etc.)
# Install the Go version
go install github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/cmd/fabric@latest
# Run setup for the new version. Important because things have changed
fabric --setup"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Uninstall Legacy Fabric</span>
pipx uninstall fabric

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Clear any old Fabric aliases</span>
(check your .bashrc, .zshrc, etc.)
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install the Go version</span>
go install github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/cmd/fabric@latest
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run setup for the new version. Important because things have changed</span>
fabric --setup</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Then <a href="#environment-variables">set your environmental variables</a> as shown above.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Upgrading</h3><a id="user-content-upgrading" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Upgrading" href="#upgrading"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The great thing about Go is that it's super easy to upgrade. Just run the same command you used to install it in the first place and you'll always get the latest version.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="go install github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/cmd/fabric@latest"><pre>go install github.com/danielmiessler/fabric/cmd/fabric@latest</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Shell Completions</h3><a id="user-content-shell-completions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Shell Completions" href="#shell-completions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fabric provides shell completion scripts for Zsh, Bash, and Fish
shells, making it easier to use the CLI by providing tab completion
for commands and options.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Zsh Completion</h4><a id="user-content-zsh-completion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Zsh Completion" href="#zsh-completion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To enable Zsh completion:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Copy the completion file to a directory in your $fpath
mkdir -p ~/.zsh/completions
cp completions/_fabric ~/.zsh/completions/

# Add the directory to fpath in your .zshrc before compinit
echo 'fpath=(~/.zsh/completions $fpath)' &gt;&gt; ~/.zshrc
echo 'autoload -Uz compinit &amp;&amp; compinit' &gt;&gt; ~/.zshrc"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Copy the completion file to a directory in your $fpath</span>
mkdir -p <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.zsh/completions
cp completions/_fabric <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.zsh/completions/

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Add the directory to fpath in your .zshrc before compinit</span>
<span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>fpath=(~/.zsh/completions $fpath)<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.zshrc
<span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>autoload -Uz compinit &amp;&amp; compinit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.zshrc</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bash Completion</h4><a id="user-content-bash-completion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bash Completion" href="#bash-completion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To enable Bash completion:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Source the completion script in your .bashrc
echo 'source /path/to/fabric/completions/fabric.bash' &gt;&gt; ~/.bashrc

# Or copy to the system-wide bash completion directory
sudo cp completions/fabric.bash /etc/bash_completion.d/"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Source the completion script in your .bashrc</span>
<span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>source /path/to/fabric/completions/fabric.bash<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.bashrc

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Or copy to the system-wide bash completion directory</span>
sudo cp completions/fabric.bash /etc/bash_completion.d/</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fish Completion</h4><a id="user-content-fish-completion" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fish Completion" href="#fish-completion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To enable Fish completion:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Copy the completion file to the fish completions directory
mkdir -p ~/.config/fish/completions
cp completions/fabric.fish ~/.config/fish/completions/"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Copy the completion file to the fish completions directory</span>
mkdir -p <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.config/fish/completions
cp completions/fabric.fish <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.config/fish/completions/</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Once you have it all set up, here's how to use it.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fabric -h"><pre>fabric -h</pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Usage:
  fabric [OPTIONS]

Application Options:
  -p, --pattern=                    Choose a pattern from the available patterns

      --session=                    Choose a session from the available sessions
